<script type="text/javascript">F.module('/static/widget/common/searchbox/searchradio.js', function(require, exports){
/*-----[ /widget/common/searchbox/searchradio.js ]-----*/
var $ = require('/static/common/ui/jquery/jquery.js');

var searchRadio = function() {
	$(function() {
        $('.search-radios').delegate('label', 'click', function() {
            var $this = $(this);

            if (willChange($this)) {
                changeBackground($this);
            }
            // var checkedId = $(this).attr('for');
            // var notCheckedId = getNotCheckedId(checkedId);

            // changeCheckedAttr(checkedId, notCheckedId);
            // changeCheckImg(checkedId, notCheckedId);
        });

        function willChange($this) {
            var isChecked = $this.hasClass('checked');
            var change = false;

            if (!isChecked) {
                change = true;
            }

            return change;
        }

        function changeBackground($this) {
            var $anotherBtn = getAnotherBtn($this);

            $this
                .removeClass('not-checked')
                .addClass('checked');

            $anotherBtn
                .removeClass('checked')
                .addClass('not-checked');
        }

        function getAnotherBtn($this) {
            var thisRadioId = $this.attr('for');    // label对应的radio的id
            var $anotherBtn;

            if (thisRadioId.indexOf('newstitle') > -1) {
                $anotherBtn = $('.search-radios label[for="news"]');   
            } else {
                $anotherBtn = $('.search-radios label[for="newstitle"]');
            }

            return $anotherBtn;
        }

        // function getNotCheckedId(checkedId) {
        //     var mark = checkedId.search('newstitle');

        //     if (mark > -1) 
        //         return 'news';
        //     else 
        //         return 'newstitle';
        // }

        // function changeCheckedAttr(checkedId, notCheckedId) {
        //     $('#' + checkedId).attr('checked', 'checked');
        //     $('#' + notCheckedId).removeAttr('checked');
        // }

        // function changeCheckImg(checkedId, notCheckedId) {
        //     $('label[for="' + checkedId + '"]').children().eq(0).css('display', '');
        //     $('label[for="' + checkedId + '"]').children().eq(1).css('display', 'none');
            
        //     $('label[for="' + notCheckedId + '"]').children().eq(0).css('display', 'none');
        //     $('label[for="' + notCheckedId + '"]').children().eq(1).css('display', '');
        // }
    });
};

exports = searchRadio;
return exports;}, ['/static/common/ui/jquery/jquery.js']);
F.module('/static/widget/common/searchbox/searchboxActive.js', function(require, exports){
/*-----[ /widget/common/searchbox/searchboxActive.js ]-----*/
var $ = require('/static/common/ui/jquery/jquery.js');

// 监听搜索框的focus状态，改变搜索框外层的边框样式
var searchboxActive = function() {

	var $searchbox = $('#ww');
	var $searchboxWrap = $('#s_ipt_wr');

	$searchbox
		.on('focus', function() {
			$searchboxWrap.addClass('focus-searchbox');
		})
		.on('blur', function() {
			$searchboxWrap.removeClass('focus-searchbox');
		});

};

exports = searchboxActive;

return exports;}, ['/static/common/ui/jquery/jquery.js']);

    <script type="text/javascript">F.module('/static/widget/common/second_navbar/fold.js', function(require, exports){
/*-----[ /widget/common/second_navbar/fold.js ]-----*/
var $ = require('/static/common/ui/jquery/jquery.js');

var fold = function() {
	$(function() {
		var $parent = $('#channel-media');
		var $ul = $('.media-row ul');

		init();

		function init() {
			showMoreBtn();
			registerFoldEvent();
		}

		// 二级导航栏只有一行时，不显示更多按钮
		function showMoreBtn() {
			var $moreBtn = $('#channel-media .media-more');
			var totalHeight = $ul.height();
			var singleHeight = $ul.find('li:eq(0)').height();

			if (totalHeight > singleHeight) {
				$moreBtn.show();
			}
		}

		function registerFoldEvent() {
			$parent.delegate('.media-row .media-more a', 'click', function() {
				var $moreBtn = $(this);
				var $ul = $('.media-row ul');
				var isFold = $moreBtn.find('i').hasClass('unfold');

				if (isFold) {
					unfold($ul);
				} else {
					fold($ul);
				}
			});
		}

		function fold($ul) {
			var $moreWrap = $('#channel-media .media-more');
			var $children = $moreWrap.children();
			var $ulWrap = $('#channel-media .media-row');
			var singleHeight = $ul.find('li:eq(0)').height();
			
			$children.eq(1).hide();
			$children.eq(0).show();
			$ulWrap.height(singleHeight);
		}

		function unfold($ul) {
			var $moreWrap = $('#channel-media .media-more');
			var $children = $moreWrap.children();
			var $ulWrap = $('#channel-media .media-row');

			$children.eq(0).hide();
			$children.eq(1).show();
			$ulWrap.css('height', 'auto');
		}
	});
};

exports = fold;
return exports;}, ['/static/common/ui/jquery/jquery.js']);

    	F.use('/static/widget/common/second_navbar/fold.js', function(fold) {
    		fold();
    	});
    </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            // 如果有图的文章出现白图的情况（图片大小小于10*10则视为白图），去掉图片展示
            function checkimg(obj){
                // console.log('obj.width: ' + obj.width);
                if(obj.naturalWidth < 10){
                    var picWrapper = obj.parentElement.parentElement;
                    var item = obj.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement;
                    // console.log('-------picWrapper');
                    // console.dir(picWrapper);
                    // console.log('-------item');
                    // console.dir(item);
                    picWrapper.style.display = 'none';
                    if (item.className.search('notb') > -1){
                        item.className = 'feeds-item-detail notb';
                    } else {
                        item.className = 'feeds-item-detail';
                    }
                }
            }
        </script>

                    UserMonitor.send(e, 6, {c: "top", a:"51", col: "4", ct: "1", m: "11", pn: 8-i});
                    window.alog && alog("monkey.fire", "record", {
                        type: "click",
                        target: item
                    }); 
                });
            });
        });
           
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var ___lis___ = $(".hotwords li"),___images___ = $('.hotwords img'),___words___=$('.hotwords_li_a');
    $.each(___images___,function(i,item){
        var $item = $(item),
        src = $item.attr('m_m_src'),
        _img = new Image();
        _img.onload = function(){

            $item.attr('src', src);
            if(_img.width > _img.height){
                if($item.parents('li').width() > 68){
                    $item.css('width', '139px');
                }else{
                    $item.css('height', '68px');

                }
            }else{
                $item.css('width',$item.parents('li').width());
            }
            _img.onload = null;
        }
        _img.src = src;
    });
    $.each(___lis___,function(i,item){
        $(item).mouseenter(function(e){
        $('.detail',this).animate({top:'0px'},200,function(){});

        });
        $(item).mouseleave(function(e){
        $('.detail',this).animate({top:'68px'},200,function(){});
        });
    });
    $.each(___words___, function(i, item) {
        $(item).find('img').length == 0 && $(item).css({"padding-top": (68 - item.offsetHeight)/2 + "px"}) || $(item).css({"padding": 0, 'width':$(item).width()+9+'px'});
        $(item).css({
            "visibility": "visible"
        });
    });
</script>

F.use(['/static/common/lib/tangram/base/base.js', '/static/widget/common/fixedpannel/fixedpannel.js'],function(baidu,feedback_init){
    /*temp for ad-for-ipad*/
    baidu.on(window,'load', function(){
        var eleTop = baidu.g("gotop_btn");
        baidu.on(window, 'scroll', function(){
            baidu.page.getScrollTop() >= 200 ? baidu.show(eleTop) : baidu.hide(eleTop);
        });
        var eleSearch = baidu.dom.query("#goTop .search")[0];
        baidu.on(eleSearch, "click", function(){
            baidu.dom.addClass(eleSearch, "show");
        });
        var eleSearchHide = baidu.dom.query("#goTop .search dd span")[0];
        baidu.on(eleSearchHide, "click", function(e){
            baidu.dom.removeClass(eleSearch, "show");
            baidu.event.stopPropagation(e);
        });
        baidu.on(document.body,"click", function(e){
            var target = baidu.event.getTarget(e);
            if(!baidu.dom.getAncestorBy(target, function(ele){return ele.id == "goTop"})){
            baidu.dom.removeClass(eleSearch, "show");
            }
        });
    feedback_init({
            tuiguang : true ,
            tuiguang_width: 564,
            tuiguang_height:429,
            tuiguang_cookiename:'NEWSNEWIPADTJ',
            tuiguang_image:'http://news.baidu.com/resource/img/tuiguang/news_home_ad_dialog_ipad_news.png',
            tuiguang_url:'https://itunes.apple.com/cn/app/id659994109?mt=8'

    });
    });
});
</script>

	function rtDealPath(path){
	    if(!path || !path.toUpperCase){
		return "";
	    }
	    var pos = path.lastIndexOf("(");
	    if(pos > -1){
		path = path.substr(pos).split(")");
		if(path.length < 2){
		    return path[0].toUpperCase();
		}
	    }
	    else{
		path = ["", path];
	    }
	    pos = path[1].lastIndexOf("C");
	    if(pos > -1){
		path[1] = path[1].split("");
		var len = path[1].length;
		pos += 1;
		while(pos <= len){
		    if(path[1][pos] <= "9" && path[1][pos] >= "0"){
			pos++;
		    }
		    else{
			break;
		    }
		}
		path[1] = path[1].slice(0, pos).join("");
	    }
	    path = path[0] ? path.join(")") : path[1];
	    return path.toUpperCase();
	}
